<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повторять.html>повторя́ть</a> (1254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повторить.html>повтори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povtorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повторять.html>повторя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povtorjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повторить.html>повтори́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to repeat, to reiterate</li>
<li>to review <i>(lesson)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повыситься.html>повы́ситься</a> (19124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повысить.html>повы́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povýsitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повыситься.html>повы́ситься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povýsitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повышаться.html>повыша́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rise, to go up, to increase</li>
<li>to advance, to improve, to heighten</li>
<li>to soar, to boom, to jump, to mount</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повысить.html>повы́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povýsitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повышаться.html>повыша́ться</a> (8623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повышать.html>повыша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povyšátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повышаться.html>повыша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povyšátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повыситься.html>повы́ситься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rise, to go up, to increase</li>
<li>to advance, to improve, to heighten</li>
<li>to soar, to boom, to jump, to mount</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повышать.html>повыша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povyšátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***повязать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повязать.html>повяза́ть</a> (8605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повязать.html>повяза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povjazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повязывать.html>повя́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повязать.html>повяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платок.html>платко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povjazátʹ</b> gólovu platkóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cover one's head with a shawl/kerchief; tie a scarf on one's head</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seize, to arrest, to bust, to nab, to pinch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повязать.html>повяза́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прямо.html>пря́мо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́мом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>povjazáli</b> prjámo péred dómom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they pinched him right in front of his house</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knit <i>(a little)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повязать.html>повяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:немного.html>немно́го</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povjazátʹ</b> nemnógo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do a little knitting; knit for a while</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***повязывавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повязывать.html>повя́зывавший</a> (29550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повязывать.html>повя́зывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povjázyvavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повязывать.html>повя́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povjázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нка</a> (15648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганый.html>пога́н</a>(ец)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pogán(ec)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нок</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганец.html>пога́нец</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> female scoundrel, scumbag, rascal</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганый.html>пога́ный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pogányj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foul</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>toadstool, poisonous mushroom
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледный.html>бле́дная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">blédnaja pogánka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">death cap, <i>Amanita phalloides</i></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>Podiceps</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">genus of waterbirds of the grebe family, whose meat has an unpleasant taste</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганка.html>пога́нка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лая</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pogánka málaja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dabchick</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поганый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поганый.html>пога́ный</a> (7264)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">поганъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poganŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pagan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paganus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pagan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поганый.html>пога́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogányj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heathen</li>
<li>foul, unclean</li>
<li>lousy, nasty, rotten</li>
<li><i>(mushroom)</i> poisonous</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пога́нить</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pogánitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">испога́нить</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ispogánitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***погасить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:погасить.html>погаси́ть</a> (5632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гасить.html>гаси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gasítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погасить.html>погаси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogasítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гасить.html>гаси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put out, to extinguish</li>
<li>to turn off (light)</li>
<li>to cancel (debt); to make invalid</li>
<li>to quench</li>
<li>to slake (lime)</li>
<li>to kill (a ball)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill, to murder, to waste; to beat</li></ol>

***погаснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:погаснуть.html>пога́снуть</a> (3684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гаснуть.html>га́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gásnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погаснуть.html>пога́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogásnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гаснуть.html>га́снуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go out (of light, fire)</li>
<li>to die away</li></ol>

***погашение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ние</a> (18349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погасить.html>погаси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pogasítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogašénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>paying off, clearing off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кций</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pogašénije</b> ákcij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">retirement of shares</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:облигация.html>облига́ций</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pogašénije</b> obligácij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">redemption of bonds</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:денежный.html>де́нежного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязательство.html>обяза́тельства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pogašénije</b> dénežnovo objazátelʹstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">meeting/redemption of a liability</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:погашение.html>погаше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кредит.html>креди́тов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pogašénije</b> kredítov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">repayment of credits</span></div></dd>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибать.html>погиба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogibátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибнуть.html>поги́бнуть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́бель</a> (11261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́бель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogíbelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́бели</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́бели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́белей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>death, destruction, ruin, perdition</li>
<li><i>in expresions only</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согнуть.html>согну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́бели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sognútʹ v tri pogíbeli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">get under one's thumb, make knuckle under</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согнуться.html>согну́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:погибель.html>поги́бели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sognútʹsja v tri pogíbeli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) double up; 2) kowtow</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:погибнуть.html>поги́бнуть</a> (918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гибнуть.html>ги́бнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gíbnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибнуть.html>поги́бнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogíbnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погибать.html>погиба́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гибнуть.html>ги́бнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to perish, to die of unnatural causes, to be killed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:погибнуть.html>поги́б</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автокатастрофа.html>автокатастро́фе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>pogíb</b> v avtokatastrófe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>was killed</b> in an auto accident</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***погладить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:погладить.html>погла́дить</a> (3992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гладить.html>гла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gláditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погладить.html>погла́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pogláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гладить.html>гла́дить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to iron, to press (clothes)</li>
<li>to pet (animals, etc.)</li>
<li>to stroke, to caress</li></ol>
